 Know important information about this communist leader
 
 
 1
 He continued to raise the voice of the working class
 iske kaaran unhen puunjipati virgon kaa kaaphi virodh bhi sahanaa padaa
 2
 fredrick angels ke saath milakar inhone 'da communist menifesto' kii rachana kii
 The concept of communism is introduced in it
 3
 Due to his revolutionary writings he was banished from Germany, France and Belgium
 4
 Marx's line 'world's workers have nothing to lose except their chains, the world's workers are one' is the slogan of every labor movement of the world even today
 5
 In 1864, Marx played a very important role in the establishment of the 'international Labor Union' in London
 6
 In the year 1867, he published the first volume of Das Capital, which is the details of his economic ideology

 7
 'vargsangharsh' kaa siddhant marks ke 'vaigyanik samaajwaad' kaa merudand he

 ) In this growing e-commerce market, the trend of online shopping is increasing

 Before starting shopping, remember that the computer must have anti-virus
 iske saath hi aaie jaanate hai online shopping ke dauraan hameshaa yaad rakhane vaali 6 baaten jo aapako kisi bhi tarah kii dhokhadhadi se bachaaengi :1
 Do not shop from unknown site
 Internet security is very important when shopping online
 iskaa matlab yah he ki aap hameshaa kisi bharose vaali site se hi kharidari karen
 If you make a payment from an unknown site, then it may be that your account is cleared within a few hours of cybercrime
 vahiin anjaan site se shopping karne par aap is rakam ko clem bhi nahin kar paaenge
 2) Understand the difference between http and https If you are shopping online, first of all, keep in mind that the address of the website from which you are buying goods should have https and not http
 yahaan is jude 'S' kaa matlab security kii guarantee se hota he
 This means that this site is not fake
 haalaankikbhi-kabhi yah 'S' letters website main tab judata he jab baari online pement karne kii aati he
 3) Check the complete information of the website, always check that the address, phone number and email address of the place where you are buying the goods are written on the website
 jahaan dhokhadhadi kii gunjaaish hoti he vahiin aksar jaankaree chhipaai jaati he
 4) Payment system Apart from this, one more thing to be noted is that you can make payment in the payment system of the website through Verified by Visa or mastercard securecode? The answer should always be yes as it helps protect you from fraud
 agar in sab jaanch parakh ke baad aap santusht hai tabhi kharidari karen
 5) Understand the terms of the company in such a manner that it is often the case that companies offer free delivery on purchases above Rs 500
 customer ko bhi yah kaaphi suvidhajanak lagata he
 But sometimes there are some conditions written along with free delivery, which the customer does not pay attention to, and because of this, they have to pay extra price later
 ye wo charge hote hai jo customer ko lubhaane ke liye shuru main bataae hi nahin jate
 6) Check the goods immediately
 Many cases have come up in which there is a lot of rigging of companies
 kai log apana order khol ke dekhte he to usamen puraani chijen yaa phir di gai jaankaree se hatakar ghatiya str kaa saamaan miltaa he
